## Wizard Lock

> **Wizard Lock**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one door, gate, hatch, chest, or similar closure **D:** permanent until dispelled or released
>
> You seal a closure with keyed arcane pressure. Opening the locked target now requires either the original key-pattern, substantial forced entry, or explicit countermagic. The lock does not reinforce the object itself; it reinforces access-state and resistance to opening.
>
> Creatures of much higher Level than you may force passage with enough time and leverage, but the entry always leaves obvious disturbance.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - apply the lock to all linked closures in a small structure (up to 3); x4 - when a locked closure is forced, you immediately sense the breach if on the same map region.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [binding]
>   [ward]
>   [imbued]

>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Wizard Lock
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wizard Lock

## Wizardry

> **Wizardry**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** self  
> **T:** one magic-user-only device or one scroll spell of 1st or 2nd level **D:** 1 turn or until discharge
>
> You borrow the operating grammar of a magic-user long enough to use one arcane device or one qualifying arcane scroll effect otherwise barred to you.
>
> While the invocation lasts, you understand the item’s activation pattern and are treated as the minimum caster level required to produce the borrowed effect.
>
> This does not let you cast 3rd-level-or-higher magic-user scroll spells, even if they appear on the scroll.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - keep the handling window open for the full duration even after one failed or interrupted activation attempt; x4 - while active, also read the operating cues of one additional magic-user-only item without discharging it.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [cross-tradition]
>   [item-use]
>   [high-tier]

> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Wizardry
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wizardry
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Wizardry; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Anti-Magic Shell

> **Anti-Magic Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self  
> **T:** self-centered personal barrier **D:** 12 turns (~2 hours)
>
> You raise a skin-tight null boundary around yourself that blocks all spell and power effects crossing the shell in either direction. Incoming powers fail at the barrier. Your own powers also cannot pass through while the shell is active.
>
> You may end the shell at will. Other than Wish-scale exception handling, ordinary countermagic cannot cancel it.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — permit one pre-declared allied support effect to pass the shell once; x4 — shell grants brief suppression pressure that forces nearby ongoing magical effects to test stability at referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [anti-magic]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

## Barrier

> **Barrier**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one cylindrical hazard field up to 30 ft diameter and 30 ft high **D:** 12 turns
>
> You establish a visible wall of whirling force-hammers that blocks passage and punishes breach attempts. Creatures that pass through take heavy impact damage with no save.
>
> The field is ideal for corridor denial, gate sealing, and forced route control.
>
> _Reverse — Remove Barrier:_ Destroy one cleric `Barrier` or one compatible wall effect (`Wall of Ice`, `Wall of Fire`, or `Wall of Stone`).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase diameter and height by 50%; x4 — barrier also imposes forced pushback on creatures that fail to cross cleanly.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [control]

## Force Field

> **Force Field**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one invisible immovable force shape up to 20 ft radius sphere or 5,000 sq ft total surface **D:** 6 turns
>
> You create a seamless barrier or object of pure force. It may take the form of a sphere, hemisphere, flat surface, cylinder, box, or part of those shapes, but it must remain perfectly smooth and regular.
>
> Nothing crosses the field by ordinary means: attacks, missiles, breath, and spells all rebound. Teleportation, Dimension Door, and planar transit can bypass it. The field cannot be broken except by Disintegrate or Wish, and even Dispel Magic cannot affect it.
>
> A sealed field preserves enclosed creatures from starvation, suffocation, and natural death while it lasts.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - refine the geometry for more exact enclosure or bridge-like support; x4 - harden one declared seam against teleport or phase bypass until the start of your next turn, unless struck by Wish-scale exception handling.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [force]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Force Field

## Contingency

> **Contingency**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature or item plus one stored non-damaging spell of 4th level or lower **D:** indefinite until triggered
>
> You bind a predeclared spell response to one specific future condition. When that exact situation next occurs, the stored spell fires immediately as though cast at that instant.
>
> The trigger may be detailed, but it must concern something within 120 ft of the triggering event. The stored spell’s target and effect must be fully specified in advance. If the trigger language is incomplete or impossible to resolve, nothing happens.
>
> No creature or item can carry more than one Contingency at a time.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - harden the trigger against interruption, disguise, or split-second ambiguity; x4 - permit one tightly specified fallback target or destination if the primary resolution state is invalid when the trigger fires.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [binding]
>   [trigger]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Contingency
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Contingency
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Contingency; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Protection from Lightning

> **Protection from Lightning**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature and carried gear **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You grant electrical damage immunity up to a finite absorption budget equal to 1d6-equivalent per user Level. Deduct incoming lightning damage dice from the pool until exhausted.
>
> While active, the target is highly resistant to lightning attacks and gains strong survival margin against storm/artillery effects.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - extend protection to one adjacent ally at reduced pool size; x4 - convert excess absorbed lightning into one retaliatory discharge action.

## Turn Wood

> **Turn Wood**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one invisible force-wave 120 ft long and 60 ft tall **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You launch a broad horizontal pressure-front that repels and captures wooden objects. The wave begins within range, immediately travels in one direction you choose at 10 ft per round, and may continue up to 360 ft total.
>
> Wooden items that touch the wave become stuck to it and move with it. Bows, spears, staves, wands, siege timber, planks, hatches, and similar objects can be displaced or rendered unusable while trapped. The wave does not harm the objects, and it does not move permanent constructions.
>
> You may stop the wave early, but once stopped it cannot move again. The stationary wave remains in place until duration ends or you dismiss it with one full round of concentration.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - spare named wooden objects or lanes from capture when placing or steering the wave; x4 - apply full displacement pressure to large wooden vehicles or siege gear not anchored as permanent structures.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [force]
>   [wood]
>   [control]
>   [druid]
>   [high-tier]

## Immunity

> **Immunity**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You weave a broad-spectrum protective field around the recipient. For the duration, the target is completely immune to all Power Level 1–6 effects (OSR spells 1st–3rd level). Power Level 7–10 effects (4th–5th level) work at half normal potency — or at one-quarter if the recipient passes a Save vs. Spells.
>
> Any quantifiable aspect of a reduced effect — damage, duration, bonuses, penalties — is halved (or quartered on a successful save). Fractions favor the protected creature.
>
> The protection also grants complete immunity to mundane and silver projectiles and to normal weapons. Magical weapons deal half damage.
>
> The recipient may drop the protection voluntarily for 1 round by concentrating, allowing beneficial effects to function normally. The field returns automatically at the start of the next round.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend full immunity to Power Level 7–8 effects and halve magical weapon damage; x4 — full immunity extends to Power Level 1–10, with reduced-immunity applying to Power Level 11+ only.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [protection]
>   [immunity]
>   [high-tier]

>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Immunity
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Immunity
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Immunity; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Mind Barrier

> **Mind Barrier**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one creature (unwilling targets may Save vs. Spells to avoid) **D:** 1 hour per user Level
>
> You raise an impenetrable lattice around the recipient’s mental presence. While the barrier holds, no form of ESP, clairvoyance, clairaudience, crystal-ball contact, or other mental surveillance or remote-influence technique can reach the target — to any such probe, the creature simply does not exist.
>
> In addition, the recipient gains +8 to all Saves against mind-influencing effects: all forms of charm, illusions, phantasms, feeblemind, and similar attacks. A natural roll of 1 always fails regardless of bonuses.
>
> _Reversible — Open Mind:_ Touch range; the target becomes fully exposed to every mind-influencing effect listed above and suffers –8 to all related Saves for the duration. Requires a successful attack roll against an unwilling target.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — the save bonus increases to +12, and one already-active dominance or charm effect is immediately suppressed; x4 — the barrier also prevents reality-manipulation attacks (geas, quest, and similar bindings) from taking hold for the duration.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [mind]
>   [protection]
>   [reversible]
>   [high-tier]

## Permanence

> **Permanence**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one active MU spell effect of 7th level or less **D:** permanent until dispelled
>
> You anchor an active magical effect in place, making it permanent until a dispel magic removes it — at normal dispel chances for the caster or a higher-level spellcaster.
>
> Constraints:
> - Cannot make permanent any effect with instantaneous or already-permanent duration (fireball, lightning bolt, disintegrate, etc.)
> - Cannot affect clerical spells or 8th- or 9th-level MU spells
> - One permanence per item or area; two maximum per creature; up to five on a weapon (each permanence on a weapon beyond the first carries a 25% noncumulative failure risk — if it fails, the weapon is destroyed)
>
> The referee decides whether any given combination is eligible; spell pairings that could destabilize a campaign should be reviewed before play.
>
> Common examples: detect magic, protection from evil, read languages, fly on creatures; light, confusion, cloudkill on areas.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — the permanence can anchor a 6th-level effect even with a shorter preparation window; x4 — a permanence failure on a weapon does not destroy it, merely wastes the casting.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [binding]
>   [duration]
>   [ritual]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Permanence
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Permanence
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Permanence; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Prismatic Wall

> **Prismatic Wall**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** a fixed point **D:** 6 turns
>
> You call into being a shimmering spectrum barrier at a fixed point within range. Choose one of two geometries at casting:
>
> - **Sphere:** A globe with 10-foot radius centered on the target point.
> - **Wall:** A flat vertical surface of up to 500 square feet, any shape, anchored to available structure.
>
> The wall is a multi-layered spectral barrier — each layer projects a different color with a distinct hazard for any creature passing through: fire, cold, lightning, petrification, transmutation, and so on, in sequence. Passing through all layers requires surviving each in turn. Attacks and spells that cross the barrier are absorbed or redirected depending on the layer struck.
>
> Creatures inside a sphere at the moment of casting are unaffected by it from the inside and may move freely within.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — duration extends to 12 turns and sphere radius rises to 20 feet; x4 — passing through any layer in the first 3 turns requires a Save vs. Death Ray in addition to the layer-specific effect.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [ward]
>   [area]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Prismatic Wall
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Prismatic Wall
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Prismatic Wall; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Symbol

> **Symbol**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one inscribed surface or a fixed mid-air point **D:** permanent (until triggered once)
>
> You inscribe a single glyph of hazardous power on any surface or in mid-air, choosing one of six types at the time of casting. The symbol cannot move; if placed on a mobile object, it remains fixed in space as the surface leaves it.
>
> **Trigger:** Any living creature that passes through, touches, or reads the rune activates it immediately with no saving throw. Exception: a magic-user (or any creature that can cast MU spells) who only reads or touches (but does not pass through) may Save vs. Spells to negate the effect for themselves.
>
> **Six symbol types:**
> - **Death** — kills any creature with 75 hp or fewer instantly.
> - **Discord** — victim attacks its nearest ally or becomes confused (as confusion) — permanent until dispelled.
> - **Fear** — victim flees at Running Speed for 30 rounds.
> - **Insanity** — victim becomes incapacitated permanently until dispelled.
> - **Sleep** — victim falls into unawakenable sleep for 1d10+10 hours or until dispelled.
> - **Stunning** — affects any creature with 150 hp or fewer; stunned for 2d6 turns.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — trigger radius extends to 10 ft, affecting all creatures within that zone when any one activates it; x4 — the symbol resets once after its first trigger, activating a total of two times before permanent discharge.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [trap]
>   [binding]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Symbol
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Symbol
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Symbol; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Geas

> **Geas**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one creature **D:** until fulfilled, removed, or the subject dies
>
> You bind a target to a specific command constraint: perform an action, complete a mission, or abstain from a defined act. The command must be possible and not directly suicidal. The target may Save vs. Spells to resist.
>
> On failure, the compulsion persists until resolved. If the subject refuses compliance, escalating penalties apply at referee call (combat penalties, weakness, reduced capability, pain, or similar collapse effects).
>
> _Reverse — Remove Geas:_ This clears an existing geas. If the remover is lower Level than the original binder, removal may fail.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — apply a -2 penalty on the target’s initial save; x4 — encode one clear completion condition that triggers immediate release when met.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [compulsion]
>   [binding]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Geas
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Geas
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Geas; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Anti-Plant Shell

> **Anti-Plant Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self  
> **T:** self-centered personal barrier **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You create an invisible skin-close barrier that blocks attacks and contact effects from plants and plant-like entities.
>
> While active, you may physically pass through dense natural growth and leave a traversable path for others. You cannot make direct physical attacks against plant targets through the barrier; spell-based interactions still function.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - brief extension to one adjacent ally inside arm’s reach; x4 - barrier also suppresses one plant-entangle or vine-control effect in contact with you.

## Anti-Animal Shell

> **Anti-Animal Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self  
> **T:** self-centered personal barrier **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You project an invisible exclusion shell that blocks attacks from normal and giant animals, insects, and other nonfantastic creatures of animal intelligence.
>
> While protected, you cannot physically attack affected creatures; both sides are mutually blocked from bodily harm through the shell unless spell-mediated.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - grant brief exclusion aura to one adjacent ally; x4 - repulse affected creatures on contact, forcing immediate retreat movement.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [barrier]
>   [animal]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:

# Creation and Conjuration

Use these for object creation, golem manufacture, simulacra, and bringing forth. Covers summons, constructs, and materialization.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Floating Disc

> **Floating Disc**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** near (2 m / 6 ft from caster)  
> **T:** one hovering force-disc **D:** 6 turns (about 1 hour)
>
> You conjure a horizontal disk of force that follows you at short distance and carries gear, salvage, or fragile cargo. The disc hovers about waist-height, follows your movement path, and cannot pass through solid barriers narrower than its footprint.
>
> The disc does not grant flight; it is a load-bearing transport surface. If forced beyond carrying limits, it collapses and drops its cargo.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase carrying capacity by one additional burden slot; x4 - create a second linked disc that follows the first.
>
> See also: `Floating Disc` in the SDM Powers Index for the existing stylized rendition.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [conjuration]
>   [utility]
>   [movement]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Floating Disc
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Floating Disc
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Floating Disc
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Floating Disc
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Floating Disc; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Wall of Stone

> **Wall of Stone**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one vertical stone wall up to 1000 cubic ft (2 ft thick) **D:** permanent until broken or dispelled
>
> You extrude shaped stone into a solid vertical barrier exactly 2 feet thick. You define the geometry freely within volume limits (for example 10 x 50 ft or 20 x 25 ft coverage), but the wall must rest on stable support and cannot appear inside occupied matter.
>
> The wall persists as real structure until physically breached or dispelled.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase total volume by 50%; x4 — add keyed apertures (ports, embrasures, or one controlled gate seam) during formation.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [barrier]
>   [infrastructure]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wall of Stone

## Create Water

> **Create Water**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one temporary spring from ground or wall **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> You call up an enchanted spring that flows from a surface or seam for about an hour. It produces enough fresh water for roughly 12 people and their mounts for a day, with additional output at higher user Levels.
>
> This is expedition infrastructure rather than combat pressure.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — double the effective daily supply output; x4 — choose a cleaner, easier-to-store flow that immediately fills nearby vessels before the rest runs free.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [water]

## Growth of Plants

> **Growth of Plants**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** up to 3000 square feet of normal plant life **D:** until reversed or dispelled
>
> You drive ordinary vegetation into dense overgrowth: vines, thorns, briars, and choking creepers erupt across a broad footprint. The result becomes impassable to all but giant-sized creatures and can close lanes, reshape approaches, or fortify camp boundaries.
>
> _Reverse — Shrink Plants:_ Collapse overgrowth back into a passable state or negate an earlier casting. This does not affect plant monsters.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase the affected area by half; x4 — the overgrowth also counts as light cover against missile fire for creatures behind it.
>
> See also: `Green Haven` for a related SDM-facing plant-shaping shelter cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [plants]
>   [terrain]

## Conjure Elemental

> **Conjure Elemental**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one elemental entity (typically 16 HD class) **D:** sustained while concentrating
>
> You call one elemental of a chosen type (earth, air, fire, or water) into active service. The elemental performs tasks within its capacity while you maintain control through continuous concentration.
>
> While maintaining control, your personal action economy is heavily constrained: you cannot cast other powers, cannot fight effectively, and cannot move faster than half speed. If control breaks, the elemental turns hostile and usually prioritizes the summoner.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — grant the elemental one temporary resistance keyed to its type while controlled; x4 — on release, dismiss cleanly without backlash even in unstable noosphere conditions.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [elemental]
>   [control]
>   [high-tier]

## Invisible Stalker

> **Invisible Stalker**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self-origin  
> **T:** one invisible stalker servitor **D:** until mission completion or destruction
>
> You summon an invisible stalker bound to complete one clearly defined mission. The servitor will pursue that task across long time and distance until complete or slain.
>
> The mission should be explicit and operationally testable (track, retrieve, guard, deliver, eliminate, or similar). Ambiguous instructions create risk of literal or hostile interpretation.
>
> `Dispel Evil` can force the stalker back to its origin plane.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — allow one contingency clause in the mission order; x4 — grant temporary noospheric trace-suppression, making the stalker harder to detect by ordinary divination.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [servitor]
>   [invisible]
>   [high-tier]

## Aerial Servant

> **Aerial Servant**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one ethereal retrieval servitor **D:** 1 day per user Level
>
> You summon an intelligent ethereal servitor and assign a single retrieval mission for one creature or item at an approximate location.
>
> The servitor can carry substantial loads (up to 5,000 cn equivalent), move through many obstacles via ethereal transit, and will continue mission execution until success, timeout, or disruption.
>
> If the mission cannot be completed before duration ends, the servitor destabilizes and may return hostile toward the summoner.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — allow one fallback retrieval condition if the primary target is unavailable; x4 — grant temporary safe-return lock, preventing hostile rebound on timeout once.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [servitor]
>   [utility]
>   [high-tier]

## Animate Objects

> **Animate Objects**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one object up to 4,000 cn or multiple smaller objects totaling that mass **D:** 6 turns
>
> You induce autonomous motion in nonliving, nonmagical objects and direct them as temporary combat or labor agents.
>
> Object behavior uses your control intent, while exact movement, defenses, and damage profile depend on size and form at referee call.
>
> Animated objects are procedural assets: statues, furniture, doors, tools, and salvage can all become short-term noospheric actuators.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase total animated mass by 50%; x4 — allow one animated object to continue a single predeclared task briefly without active command.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [animation]
>   [control]
>   [utility]
>   [high-tier]

## Clone

> **Clone**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one prepared flesh sample and growth vessel **D:** permanent; growth usually 1 week per HD
>
> You grow a duplicate body from harvested living tissue. For humans and demihumans, the result is a true clone: a nonmagical duplicate that awakens as the original existed when the tissue was taken.
>
> If the original is already dead when the clone matures, the clone wakes as a restored earlier self. If both original and clone live on the same plane, a dangerous mind-link forms: shared pain, mutual awareness, and an overwhelming drive in the clone to destroy the original. Failure to resolve that conflict leads to insanity and can end in permanent, unrecoverable death.
>
> Non-humanoid results are simulacra instead: obedient enchanted duplicates with partial traits that can improve if the original is dead. Constructs and undead cannot be cloned.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - harden the growth chamber against tampering and casual detection during maturation; x4 - reinforce cross-planar separation so a matured clone kept off-plane remains link-stable until brought onto the original’s plane.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [body]
>   [deathless]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Clone
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Clone
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Clone; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Create Normal Animals

> **Create Normal Animals**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one large, three medium, or six small normal animals **D:** 10 turns
>
> You instantiate loyal normal animals at a chosen nearby point. They obey commands, can fight, carry loads, and perform practical tasks to the limit of their nature.
>
> You choose quantity class (large/medium/small), while exact species is referee-selected unless campaign doctrine says otherwise.
>
> Created animals vanish when slain or when duration ends.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend command range and improve initial obedience under chaos pressure; x4 — allow mixed-size grouping within the same total output budget.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [animal]
>   [summon]
>   [high-tier]

## Create Any Monster

> **Create Any Monster**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** far (~27 m / 90 ft)  
> **T:** created creatures totaling up to your Level in HD, or one prepared construct **D:** 3 turns; permanent for construct outcome
>
> You fabricate one or more nonhuman, nondemihuman creatures from noospheric pattern and force. Total created Hit Dice cannot exceed your Level.
>
> Creatures with three or more special abilities require prior study of a matching specimen for at least one hour. Created monsters can be blocked by Protection from Evil or Anti-Magic Shell effects.
>
> You may instead create one construct if you supply the proper materials. That construct is permanent rather than temporary, though still vulnerable to normal dispelling. Constructs with four or more special abilities usually double the already severe material cost.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - reinforce initial command stability and reduce first-round confusion in a mixed monster group; x4 - improve construct cohesion so one created construct resists the first hostile disruption check or adverse control wobble.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [monster]
>   [construct]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Create Any Monster
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Create Any Monster
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Create Any Monster; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Create Magical Monsters

> **Create Magical Monsters**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** created creatures totaling up to your Level in HD, or one prepared two-asterisk construct **D:** 2 turns; permanent for construct outcome
>
> You fabricate temporary monsters with limited special abilities, choosing the creatures and bringing them into being out of thin air. Total created Hit Dice cannot exceed your Level.
>
> This version can produce monsters with up to two special abilities and may include undead, but never humans or demihumans. As with the lesser creation suite, created monsters vanish when duration ends.
>
> If you supply the proper materials, you may instead create one permanent construct with no more than two special abilities. Such constructs remain vulnerable to normal dispelling.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - improve obedience and coordination across the created group’s first exchange; x4 - reinforce one created construct so it ignores the first morale break, command wobble, or hostile disruption pressure it would suffer.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [monster]
>   [construct]
>   [high-tier]

## Summon Animals

> **Summon Animals**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~110 m / 360 ft)  
> **T:** one or more normal animals totaling up to your Level in HD **D:** 3 turns
>
> You call nearby normal animals to your side and befriend them for the duration. They come at best speed, understand your speech, and help within the limit of their nature.
>
> If harmed, a summoned animal usually flees unless it arrived into an active fight on your behalf.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - refine the summons to preferred species groups or task profile; x4 - maintain morale steadiness even after first harm check.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]

>   [animal]

## Summon Elemental

> **Summon Elemental**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one 16 HD elemental **D:** 6 turns
>
> You summon one elemental of a chosen type and bind it to understand and follow spoken commands within its capabilities.
>
> Druidic advantage: unlike the standard magic-user pattern, this version does not require ongoing concentration to maintain control. The caster may dismiss the elemental with a command; hostile countermagic can also send it back.
>
> Daily cap: usually one of each elemental type per day.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - reinforce obedience against turbulence or contested command pressure; x4 - allow one enhanced task envelope such as coordinated hauling, breach work, or battle-line shaping.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [elemental]
>   [druid]
>   [high-tier]

## Sticks to Snakes

> **Sticks to Snakes**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** up to 2d8 sticks or similar wooden shafts **D:** 6 turns
>
> You transform 2d8 sticks (arrows, staffs, branches, kindling bundles) into living snakes that obey spoken commands. Each snake has a 50% chance of being venomous (roll 1d6 per snake; 1–3 = venomous, 4–6 = non-venomous). Snakes attack and act on your initiative.
>
> When slain or when the duration expires, snakes revert to inert sticks.
>
> Snakes: AC 6, HD 1, 1 bite for 1d4 + possible venom; MV 90’ (30’); ML 12.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase the snake count to 3d8; x4 — all snakes produced are venomous and their venom requires a Save vs. Poison or the victim is paralyzed for 1d4 rounds in addition to damage.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [transformation]
>   [cleric]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Sticks to Snakes

## Clothform

> **Clothform**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** touch
> **T:** nonliving space up to 30’ x 30’ cloth volume **D:** permanent
>
> You extrude and shape non-magical cloth from noospheric patterning into mundane matter. The created material is ordinary cloth (often like undyed linen), but it is permanent and non-dispellable.
>
> With craft skill, you may shape the cloth while forming it: sail, tent, garment, drape, or rope-length equivalents. Multiple castings can be joined seamlessly edge-to-edge.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - double area to two linked 30’ x 30’ sheets. x4 - create fitted functional geometry (rigging, layered weather shelter, or stitched compartments) without additional mundane assembly.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]

## Wall of Iron

> **Wall of Iron**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)
> **T:** one supported iron wall up to 500 sq ft, 2’ thick **D:** permanent
>
> You create a vertical iron wall on valid support. The wall ignores most direct spell damage and endures until disintegrated, broken by massive force, or neutralized by special counters.
>
> If toppled, it crashes for catastrophic impact damage and shatters. Rust monsters and comparable corrosion vectors can destroy it rapidly.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - allow a hinged or angled geometry while preserving total area. x4 - wall gains temporary anti-collapse stabilization for one scene.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [barrier]
>   [metal]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Wall of Iron
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wall of Iron
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Wall of Iron; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Create Normal Monsters

> **Create Normal Monsters**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)
> **T:** summoned non-special monsters totaling user Level in HD **D:** 1 turn
>
> You instantiate temporary mundane monster-forces that obey your commands for one turn, then vanish with all carried gear.
>
> Total summoned Hit Dice cannot exceed your user Level. Chosen monsters must be non-special entries (no special ability marker), and cannot be humans, demihumans, or undead.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - extend duration by 1 additional turn. x4 - permit one restricted tactical trait (formation drilling, coordinated guarding, or hauling discipline) for the summoned group.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [control]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Create Normal Monsters

## Summon Object

> **Summon Object**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** infinite
> **T:** one prepared nonliving object (<= 500 cn) **D:** instantaneous retrieval
>
> You recall one pre-marked object from your home locus directly into your hand, even across planar boundaries.
>
> The object must be pretreated with costly summoning powder and you must know its exact placement. Only one prepared object can be summoned per cast.
>
> If another being currently possesses the object, summon fails but you receive approximate bearer location sense.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - summon up to two linked prepared components from the same storage locus. x4 - bypass one intervening anti-theft ward of moderate strength.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [utility]

meta:

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Summon Object
> - usage:

# Undead and the Deathless

Use these for death magic, necromancy, undead command, and life-force manipulation. Covers resurrection, undead animation, and death-adjacent powers.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Dispel Evil

> **Dispel Evil**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** undead, enchanted entities, one curse, or one charm field **D:** 1 turn (for concentration-driven repel)
>
> You project focused counter-sanctification against undead, summoned, controlled, or animated hostile entities. Affected targets Save vs. Spells or are destroyed/banished by class.
>
> If cast against one target only, that target takes a -2 save penalty. Even on successful saves, affected entities must withdraw while you maintain concentration.
>
> Alternate use: remove one curse from an item or clear one magical charm influence.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase effective repel radius and hold pressure while concentrating; x4 — one failed target is forcibly expelled with no retreat opportunity.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [banishment]
>   [undead]
>   [high-tier]

meta:

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Dispel Evil
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Dispel Evil; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Holy Word

> **Holy Word**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** self-centered burst (40 ft / 12 m radius)  
> **T:** all creatures in the burst **D:** instant plus condition duration by target tier
>
> You release a sanctified command-syllable that strikes all non-aligned creatures in the area with tiered consequence severity. Targets of your own alignment are unaffected.
>
> Effect severity follows target power tier: low-tier foes may be slain outright; mid-tier foes are stunned; higher-tier foes are deafened or briefly stunned. High-tier or resilient targets may Save vs. Spells to negate.
>
> The utterance propagates through most solid barriers and is blocked only by lead, anti-magic shell conditions, or equivalent suppression.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase radius to 60 ft / 18 m; x4 - one failed target of your choice is also banished or force-routed from immediate engagement, referee permitting.
>
> See also: `Sense Allegiance` as an SDM ethical-targeting cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [word]
>   [banishment]
>   [undead]
>   [high-tier]

> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Holy Word; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Raise Dead

> **Raise Dead**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one dead human or demihuman body **D:** permanent
>
> You restore life to a dead human, dwarf, elf, or halfling body within the spell’s death-age limit. Missing body parts remain missing and impose lasting disability until separately resolved.
>
> The restored subject returns with 1 Life, severe recovery restrictions, and reduced function until extended bed rest completes. This recovery cannot be accelerated by ordinary magic unless a stronger resurrection tier is used.
>
> Offensive clause: cast against undead, this power forces a Save vs. Spells at -2 or destroys the target; exceptional undead may instead be routed or partially neutralized.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - improve immediate post-return stability (reduced collapse risk in first scene); x4 - grant one short recovery acceleration step, reducing downtime burden at referee-approved scale.
>
> See also: `Raise Dead` (UVG2e) and `Recall Soul` as related SDM precedents.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [restoration]
>   [resurrection]
>   [undead]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Raise Dead
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Raise Dead
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Raise Dead
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Recall Soul
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Raise Dead; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Raise Dead Fully

> **Raise Dead Fully**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one dead creature body (full human/demihuman recovery; broader living creatures by stricter limits) **D:** permanent
>
> You perform high-tier full resurrection. Human and demihuman recipients return immediately at full Life and normal function, retaining pre-death afflictions unless separately cured.
>
> For non-human/demihuman living creatures, harsher Raise Dead-style limits apply.
>
> Anti-undead clause: destroys weaker undead outright, heavily pressures mid-tier undead saves, and deals heavy damage to stronger undead.
>
> _Reverse — Obliterate:_ Inverts the effect for lethal anti-living application and restorative anti-undead inversion behavior by doctrine.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [resurrection]
>   [undead]
>   [high-tier]
>   [reversible]

## Animate Dead

> **Animate Dead**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one or more intact corpses or skeletal remains **D:** permanent until destroyed or released
>
> You call corpse-matter into a hostile motion state, raising skeletons or zombies under your command. Raised undead follow direct orders and defend themselves if uncontrolled, but they are mindless and interpret commands literally.
>
> You may control total undead Hit Dice up to roughly twice your Level through this power; beyond that, older creations go feral, dormant, or hostile at referee call.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - raise one additional corpse in the same activation; x4 - grant raised undead a brief coordinated action burst on the round they rise.
>
> See also: `Animate Corpse` in the SDM Powers Index for a close descendant variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:item]
>   [necromancy]
>   [summon]
>   [control]
>   [dangerous]

# FTLS Powers

These magitech (oldtech) and sorcery (fantascience) Powers are practiced by the fae tribes and clans of Elyncia. If tagged with a Heritage, characters with good factional standing can purchase them at a 50% discount from friendly factions that know these Powers.

Heritage-origin recognizers now indexed under OSR sections: `Swamp's Gift (Water Breathing)` in Traversal and Mobility, and `Veilwalk (Passwall)` in Dimensional, Planar, and Exotic Access.

Avatar of the Dream, Summon Guardian Spirit, Breath Weapon, Dream Pounce, Enchanting Melody, Elemental Gift, Psychedelic Veil, Shadowform, Laughing Curse, Echo Memory, Prey-Binder, and Flow-Arts — katas and jurus codified as balance, strike, and footwork forms taught from youth.

All spider folk clans share three heritage powers (Level 1 rites): **Cast Web** (craft snares or silk resources), **Leap** (double jump distance for a scene), **Swarm Sense** (summon swarm creature once per watch).

**Swarm Sense** – Once per watch, you may call or dismiss rodents (rats, mice, squirrels) within Level \+ Thought × 10 yd.

* They gather to provide **advantage on Recon or Salvage rolls** for 1 day.

* If these rolls botch (natural 1) they scatter or panic — you must make an Aura Save to avoid being nipped, harried, or fatigued.

 Master (choose at the moment you trigger it, once/scene):  
 *Stampede*: Rush up to your Speed through enemies; each must Save or be shoved 1 square and shaken (–1) for a round.  
 *Brush Phantom*: Immediately Hide (even in light cover) and Dash (move up to Speed without provoking reactions); your next attack from hiding has Advantage.

Grave-Wrought Gift, Crown of the Grave, Soul Anchor

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Temporarily re-sculpt your limbs or integrated armor plates into tools or weapons for 10 minutes.
>
> Heritages:
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

## Assimilation Protocol

> **Assimilation Protocol**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Heritages: Awakened Vome
>
>
>
> Once per watch, initiate a link handshake with a machine, construct, vome, or cybernetic organism within (Level \+ Thought) × 10 yd. The target must choose:
>
> * **Accept** — You both gain \+1 to all rolls involving each other for the next watch and may share Power points freely while within sight of each other.
> * **Refuse** — Target makes an **Attrition (Wear & Tear) Save**. On a fail, they lose 1 Endurance or Aura. If they cannot lose Endurance or Aura, they suffer Wear and Tear instead: maximum Life is reduced by Level, and the wear occupies a Burden slot until removed.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [oldtech]
>   [storage:burden]
>   [totem]
>   [vome]
>   [stance]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Assimilation Protocol; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Avatar of the Dream

> **Avatar of the Dream**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** Self; effects extend to nearby nodes/glyphs in the local Nexus  
> **T:** Self; plus up to (Level) nearby allies for linked actions **D:** One scene, or until ended as noted below
>
> Once per watch, root your psychic self into the local Noösphere as a free action. While rooted, your body becomes an awakened locus: you gain \+1 Armor and \+1 Ward, perceive hidden dream-structures and ley-patterns, and can interface with the region’s dream-code. While in this state you may, as free actions:
>
> * Mind-Surf — You and up to (Level) nearby allies transmit your spiritual bodies through a nearby node or spirit glyph to another connected node within the Nexus (destination set by Referee or via a successful Arcane Alignment check). Your physical bodies remain at the locus.
> * Backrooms Access — You and up to (Level) nearby allies teleport physically up to (Level \+ Charisma) × 20 yd to a location your locus-sense can validly trace. Using Backroom Access ends the Dream state.
>
> End Conditions: The Dream state ends early if you move your physical body more than 5 yd, if you use Backroom Access (unless x4 overcharged as above), or if you make a Defeat roll.
>
> _Overcharge:_ *x2* — ally limit becomes (Level \+ Thought); Backroom Access distance becomes (Level \+ Charisma) × 40 yd. *x4* — you may use Backroom Access once without ending the Dream state; Mind-Surf can jump through two connected nodes in a chain.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [anchored]
>   [concentration]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Avatar of the Dream; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Battle Shell

> **Battle Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 1\. **R:** Self; aura 2 yd for ally cover.  
> **T:** Self (stance) and adjacent allies. **D:** While braced and until you move willingly.
>
> Requires a braced posture.
>
> Enter a braced stance; gain \+2 Defense, and ignore “shove/knock prone” effects that don’t also deal damage. Adjacent allies gain \+1 Defense while you remain braced. Enemies treat your zone as difficult terrain unless they beat a Strength test. Your shell becomes a temporary strongpoint — a caravan might even pitch a tent against you and feel safe.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — \+3 Defense while braced; x4 — adjacent allies also gain \+1 Defense.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [oldtech]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [focus]
>   [stance]
>   [defense]

## Breaker of Waves

> **Breaker of Waves**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 1\. **R:** (Level \+ Charisma) × 10 yd aura centered on you.  
> **T:** You and allies in aura. **D:** One crossing of the specified hazard (or 10 minutes, whichever is shorter).
>
> Effect: Once per watch, ignore difficult water, surf, sludge, or slick ice and grant Advantage on one roll to cross the same obstacle (including with mounts/vehicles).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — ignore difficult terrain from rain, sleet, or grease-like effects; x4 — vehicles and mounts also gain \+2 to relevant control checks.

## Burrower’s Instinct

> **Burrower’s Instinct**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 1 **R:** 30 × 30 yd patch of natural ground (or native stone).  
> **T:** The surveyed area; self for the skill bonus. **D:** Mapping is instantaneous; the Recon bonus lasts one watch.
>
> Spend 1 power to nose-map the ground, detecting void pockets, newly-dug passages, and pressure-weak zones. You also gain Advantage on Recon checks about stonework, cave-ins, or tunnel stability for one watch.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — double the mapped footprint; x4 — also detect thin void membranes and dormant sinkholes.

>

>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — gain \+1 Armor and Advantage on Swim checks for the duration; x4 — also gain passive water-sense within 10 yd (detects currents/large moving creatures).

## Crown of the Grave

> **Crown of the Grave**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** (Level \+ Thought) × 10 yd.  
> **T:** Each undead in range (choose individually). **D:** One watch.
>
> Declare your claim over nearby undead. Each target chooses:
>  • Accept — You and that undead gain \+1 to all rolls involving each other for the duration; you may share Power freely while within sight.
>  • Refuse — Target makes an Attrition (Wear & Tear) Save. On a fail, they lose 1 Endurance or Aura; if they cannot, they suffer Wear & Tear instead (max Life reduced by Level, fill 1 Burden slot until removed). Price: 2 Life (modified by Affinity).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — add “Disoriented” to Refusers for 1 round on a failed save; x4 — you also gain passive sense of each affected target’s location in range.

## Dream-Skim

> **Dream-Skim**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self (plus aura 10 yd for detection) **D:** 1 minute (concentration)
>
> You flutter at the edges of waking, dipping into the shared dream-stream that seeps through all nearby minds. For one minute you sense the presence of conscious or dreaming creatures within the aura, even through walls or darkness, though not their exact form or identity. With focus, you may glean a surface impression — fear, hunger, rage, or serenity — though strong wards or iron taboos may block this. At higher overcharge you can pierce deeper: ×2 expands your net wider, while ×4 pulls you into a target’s dreamscape, exposing you to both truths and nightmares until the scene ends.
>
> _Overcharge:_ ×2 — extend aura to 30 yd; ×4 — enter shared dream of one target in range for one scene.

>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [concentration]
>   [dream]
>   [shadow]
>   [psychic]
>   [scout]

## Earthshaker

> **Earthshaker**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Stomp or strike the ground with force:
>
> * All creatures within 10 yards must Save (Endurance):
>   * **Fail**: knocked prone and take 1d6 damage.
>   * **Success**: momentarily staggered—treat as Disoriented for 1 round (−1 to all rolls).
> * If underground or in a structurally unstable area, roll 1d6: on a 1, a hazard or collapse is triggered (Referee decides).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [earth]
>   [totem]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Earthshaker; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

> **Echo Memory**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Once per watch (4 hours), enter a meditative trance to witness a single memory fragment left in the dream-shadows of a place or object (Referee discretion). Save or suffer psychic backlash (1d4 Thought damage with temporary disorientation).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

## Echolocation Pulse

> **Echolocation Pulse**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** here (aura 20 yd)  
> **T:** zone (all within aura) **D:** 1 round
>
> Heritages: Bat Folk
>
>
>
> You let loose a rapid series of squeaks and trills, painting the world in echoes. For one round you gain blindsight within the aura, automatically perceiving hidden or invisible creatures, concealed doors, or traps that rely on moving parts. Foes hiding or cloaked in the zone must roll a save (Agility vs. your Thought) or be revealed to all allies for that round. The pulse does not carry through silence fields or heavy sound-dampening wards, and it may alert nearby creatures attuned to vibration.
>
> _Overcharge:_ ×2 — extend aura to 40 yd; ×4 — pierce solid barriers up to 5 yd thick.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [totem]
>   [sound]
>   [shadow]
>   [scout]

>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>

>
> * **Success**: resume normal size without harm.
> * **Failure**: suffer 1 Endurance or Aura damage, or a Wear and Tear burden.
>

## Grave-Wrought Gift

> **Grave-Wrought Gift**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 0 (triggered edge case). **R:** Self.  
> **T:** Self. **D:** Instantaneous (when reduced to 0 Life).
>
>  Effect: When you hit 0 Life, immediately cast one Power you know. If you have no Life to spend, pay its price in Ability score points instead (1 point \= 1 Life). If you cannot pay the full cost, the Power fails. Referee may call for a danger roll if applicable.
>
> _Overcharge:_ n/a.

## Laughing Curse

> **Laughing Curse**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Once per watch, unleash a hyena-laugh that echoes through fear itself. Enemies within (Level \+ Charisma) × 10 yards must make an Aura save:
>
> * Success: no effect.
> * Fail: flee or fall prone (referee chooses).
>
> If at least one enemy fails this Save, and you are a Player Daemon with a Hero Die pool, gain \+1 Hero Die. (If used by a non-Daemon NPC, treat the Hero Die as a 1-use bonus die usable within the scene.)
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

## Mist-Woven Hide

> **Mist-Woven Hide**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** Self  
> **T:** Self **D:** Up to 10 minutes, or until you end it (free action)
>
> Once per watch you may dissolve into swirling fog, becoming a semi-intangible mist (as Amorphous Body). You occupy your space, carry worn/held gear, and move normally, but you can’t perform fine manipulation or speak clearly. You can slip through narrow openings and cannot be pinned by effects that require firm purchase. Area effects and magic affect you normally. You lightly obscure your own space; gain Advantage on Stealth in dim light, smoke, or natural mist.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — While misted, gain \+2 Defense and Advantage on saves vs. grapple/restraints; you can seep through gaps ≥ 4 in/10 cm; x4 — You can seep through hairline cracks; you’re immune to grapple/shove, and nonmagical weapon attacks deal half damage to you.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [oldtech]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [water]
>   [totem]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft

## Myrmidon Surge

> **Myrmidon Surge**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** nearby (aura 10 yd)  
> **T:** each willing ally in aura (see modes **D:** 1 round
>
> Heritages: Ant Folk,
>
>
>
> You snap a drilled call/beat/volley that pulls bodies into one mind. Choose one mode when you cast:
>
> * **Onslaught:** Allies in the aura gain **\+2 to their first attack roll** this round. Once this round, if **two or more attached Units** in the aura have hits on the same target, you may resolve their damage as a **single Focused source** (Volley-style) **without spending a Command Die**.
> * **Phalanx:** Allies in the aura gain **\+2 Defense** until the start of your next turn. Once this round, **one attached Unit** in the aura may **Brace without being marked** (no tempo debt).
>
> The signal’s style varies by culture (shield-clash, chant, pheromone click), but the effect is the same: lanes open, shields lock, and the line moves as one.
>
> _Overcharge:_ ×2 — aura 20 yd; ×4 — apply both modes below instead of choosing one.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [fantascience]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [command]
>   [tactics]
>   [rite]
>   [network]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Myrmidon Surge; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Overmind Link

> **Overmind Link**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 (networked action economy \+ remote casting is potent). **R:** 1 mile.  
> **T:** You and up to (Level) allied constructs (including Vome). **D:** One watch; ends early if you voluntarily sever the link.
>
> Heritages: Awakened Vome
>
>  Effect: Merge thoughts; all linked share sensory input and mental Ability scores. Any Power you cast may originate from any linked body in the mesh. Price: 3 Life to initiate (modified by Affinity), then 1 Life per watch to maintain.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — also link 1 non-construct ally per 2 Levels; x4 — range becomes 5 miles along active DreamNet paths.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]

> - source:

## Pheromone Beacon

> **Pheromone Beacon**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 1 **R:** here (trail along your path; aura 20 yd to read it)  
> **T:** this zone (allies within aura) **D:** scene (or until washed away)
>
> Heritages: Ant Folk
>
>
> You exude an invisible scent-code that binds to air currents and surfaces, leaving a persistent trail allies can sense within the aura. For the duration, allies who can read your pheromones gain advantage on checks to **track, regroup, or navigate back** along your route and cannot become **lost** by normal means in that zone. Hostiles can’t perceive the code unless they possess a comparable pheromone sense or relevant power. Heavy rain, strong solvents, or a silence-like field for scent will break the trail early.
>
> _Overcharge:_ ×2 — aura 40 yd and lasts one watch; ×4 — also spoofs a false trail that imposes disadvantage on enemy tracking for one scene.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [network]
>   [scent]
>   [scout]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Pheromone Beacon; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Shell Craft

> **Shell Craft**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 1 (baseline refit); complex refits see Overcharge. **R:** Self; touch items.  
> **T:** Your shell and attached gear/foci/harnesses. **D:** Until removed or damaged.
>
> Fueled by time, tools, and materials: 1 power per hour of work per Stone of gear integrated.
>
> Affix gear, ritual foci, shields, or quick-deploy harnesses directly to your shell; redesign and reinforce your retrofits as needed. Treat attached items as ready to draw/activate; referee may grant Advantage on “draw/brace” style actions that leverage the mounting.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — complete a complex retrofit in 10 minutes instead of 1 hour; x4 — add a “shell Inventory” to the character with one gear slot per hour spent (Skilled limit 3, Expert Limit 6, Master limit 9).

tags:
>   [power]
>   [oldtech]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [fueled]
>   [craft]
>   [shell]

## Soul Anchor

> **Soul Anchor**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 (strong persistence effect). **R:** Touch (to bind); re-form occurs at the anchor.  
> **T:** A fixed object, site, or relic. **D:** Permanent until destroyed or ritually unbound.
>
> Fixed Object, Site, or Relic: locks 4 Life essence into the anchor. Your essence remains locked until you voluntarily unbind (1 hour) or the anchor is destroyed.
>
> Bind your spirit to the anchor. You cannot be permanently destroyed unless the anchor is destroyed. When reduced to 0 Life reform at the anchor after 1d6 minutes with half maximum Life. Use this 1/day, or recharge by spending a Hero Die.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — anchor can be moved with a 1-hour rite; x4 — when reforming, also clear 1 Burden.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [necromancy]
>   [anchor]
>   [persistence]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Soul Anchor; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

## Summon Guardian Spirit

> **Summon Guardian Spirit**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Once per session, call forth a guardian of bark and basalt from a shrine, ley-node, or elemental vein. The area becomes “Awakened” in the DreamNet.
>
> * Guardian Spirit: Level 3, Life 16, \+5 to actions, 1d6+3 damage, \+3 Armor/+3 Ward.
> * Duration: 1 watch (4 hours) or until defeated. When the spirit binding ends, make a Danger Roll vs Power spent.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Surge

> **Surge**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** 15-yd cone  
> **T:** Creatures in cone **D:** Instantaneous, with knockback resolution
>
> Unleash a crashing wave. Creatures in the cone take 2d6\* damage and must Save (Endurance) or be knocked prone and pushed 1d6\* yd away from you. On a successful Save, they take half damage and are not pushed or knocked prone. Price: 3 Life (Affinity may reduce by 1, minimum 1).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — deal \+1d6\* damage and push an additional 1d6\* yd; x4 — cone extends to 25 yd and targets make their save at Disadvantage.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [water]
>   [attack]
>   [control]

## Thunder Step

> **Thunder Step**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> Dash 20 yd without provoking reactions and crackle with harmless lightning for one round.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [chaos]
>   [lightning]

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Venom Bolt

> **Venom Bolt**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** short  
> **T:** self **D:** instant
>
> The mage summons the overflowing love for all things into their Heart Chakra (green, center of chest), then cruelly inverts it and casts it towards their community’s enemy. On a successful Charisma attack deal 1d6 life Damage and 1 point of Endurance damage. If they take any damage the target must make an Endurance save. On a failed save they take 1 point of life damage (venom) at the end of their turn for the next 1d6 rounds.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — standard escalation per referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [ritual]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [venom]
>   [gaze]

meta:
> - source:

> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Venom Bolt; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Warren-Soul

> **Warren-Soul**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** 1 zone you can reasonably enclose/define as “warren” (camp, cave, ship compartment).  
> **T:** The chosen place; allies within. **D:** Until dawn or until you leave the area for a full watch.
>
> Once per day, declare a “home warren.” Allies inside gain \+1 to saves vs fear and environmental hazards. You always know the shortest path back to the warren and can squeeze your body through any passage that a Small creature could manage (you contort like a seasoned burrower).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — also grants \+1 Defense inside; x4 — you may designate two small connected zones as one warren.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [ritual]
>   [storage:trait]
>   [earth]
>   [ward]
>   [rite]

meta:
> - source:
>   - book: Flying_Triremes_and_Laser_Swords_06_Powers_and_ECM; page: working-draft
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Warren-Soul; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.
